â”œâ”€â”€ 9.1 TELOMERE STRUCTURE
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.1.1 Composition
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TTAGGG repeats (5-15kb in humans)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 3' G-rich overhang
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ T-loop: Protective structure
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ G-quadruplex formation
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.1.2 Shelterin Complex
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TRF1, TRF2: Double-strand binding
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POT1: Single-strand (overhang)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TIN2, TPP1, RAP1: Bridging
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Protects from DNA damage response
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 9.1.3 End Replication Problem
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ DNA polymerase can't copy 5' end
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ ~50-200bp lost per division
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ Replicative senescence trigger
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 9.2 TELOMERASE
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.2.1 Components
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TERT: Catalytic subunit (reverse transcriptase)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TERC: RNA template component (451 nt)
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Accessory proteins: DKC1, NOP10, etc.
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.2.2 Mechanism
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TERC provides template (AAUCCC)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TERT extends 3' overhang
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Repeat addition processivity
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ C-strand filled by primase/polymerase
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.2.3 Expression Pattern
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Active: Stem cells, germ cells
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Repressed: Most somatic cells
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Reactivated: ~90% of cancers
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ âš ï¸ Immortality target!
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 9.2.4 Hayflick Limit
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ ~50-70 divisions for human fibroblasts
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Telomere-dependent senescence
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ Can be bypassed with TERT
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 9.3 TELOMERE MEASUREMENT
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.3.1 qPCR Method
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ T/S ratio: Telomere/Single-copy gene
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Fast, cheap, scalable
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Relative measurement
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.3.2 TRF (Terminal Restriction Fragment)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Southern blot-based
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Absolute length (kb)
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Gold standard but labor-intensive
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.3.3 Flow-FISH
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Flow cytometry + FISH
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Single-cell resolution
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Cell subpopulation analysis
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 9.3.4 TeSLA
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Single telomere length analysis
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Detects critically short
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ Most sensitive
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 9.4 TELOMERE EXTENSION STRATEGIES âš ï¸
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.4.1 AAV-TERT Gene Therapy
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Deliver TERT via AAV vector
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Transient expression safer
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Buss et al. mouse studies
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.4.2 CRISPRa TERT Activation
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Endogenous TERT activation
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Precise control possible
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Your target approach!
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 9.4.3 Small Molecules
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ TA-65: Telomerase activator
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GRN510: TERT transcription
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Evidence weak but promising
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 9.4.4 Safety Considerations
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Cancer risk: Must balance!
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Tissue-specific expression
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Time-limited activation
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ Careful monitoring required
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 9.5 ALT (Alternative Lengthening of Telomeres)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Telomerase-independent
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Recombination-based
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ ~10% of cancers use ALT
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ATRX/DAXX mutations common
â”‚

â”œâ”€â”€ 10.1 DNA METHYLATION
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.1.1 Mechanism
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 5-methylcytosine (5mC) at CpG sites
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ ~28 million CpGs in human genome
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ CpG islands: Promoter-associated, mostly unmethylated
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Gene silencing correlation
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.1.2 DNA Methyltransferases
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ DNMT1: Maintenance methylation
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ DNMT3A/B: De novo methylation
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ TET enzymes: Demethylation (5mC â†’ 5hmC)
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 10.1.3 Aging Changes âš ï¸
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Global hypomethylation
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Promoter hypermethylation
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Loss of methylation fidelity
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ Epigenetic drift
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 10.2 HISTONE MODIFICATIONS
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.2.1 Types
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Acetylation (Ac): Generally activating
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ H3K27ac, H3K9ac
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ HATs add, HDACs remove
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Methylation (Me): Context-dependent
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ H3K4me3: Activating (promoters)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ H3K27me3: Repressive (Polycomb)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ H3K9me3: Heterochromatin
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Other: Phosphorylation, ubiquitination
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.2.2 Chromatin States
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Euchromatin: Open, active
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Heterochromatin: Closed, silent
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ChromHMM: State annotation
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 10.2.3 Aging Changes âš ï¸
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Loss of H3K9me3 (heterochromatin loss)
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Altered H3K27me3 landscapes
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ SIRT deacetylases decline
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 10.3 EPIGENETIC CLOCKS âš ï¸
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.3.1 Horvath Multi-tissue Clock (2013)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 353 CpG sites
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Works across tissues, species
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ MAE ~3.6 years
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Measures "epigenetic age"
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.3.2 GrimAge (2019)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Predicts mortality/morbidity
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Based on DNAm surrogates
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Includes smoking, plasma proteins
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Better mortality prediction
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.3.3 PhenoAge
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Based on clinical biomarkers
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Predicts phenotypic age
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.3.4 DunedinPACE
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Measures RATE of aging
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Not absolute age
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ More responsive to interventions
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 10.3.5 Implementation
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Illumina 450K/EPIC arrays
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Î²-values: Methylation level (0-1)
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ ElasticNet regression
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ 10.4 PARTIAL REPROGRAMMING âš ï¸
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.4.1 Yamanaka Factors
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ OSKM: Oct4, Sox2, Klf4, Myc
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Full reprogramming â†’ iPSCs
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Resets epigenetic age to ~0
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.4.2 Partial/Transient Reprogramming
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Short OSKM exposure
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Rejuvenation WITHOUT full dedifferentiation
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ OSK (no Myc): Safer

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 10.4.3 Delivery Methods
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ AAV vectors
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ mRNA (transient)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Small molecules (future)
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Inducible systems (doxycycline)
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 10.4.4 Safety Concerns
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Cancer risk (especially Myc)
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Teratoma formation

â”œâ”€â”€ 11.1 VIRAL VECTORS
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 11.1.1 AAV (Adeno-Associated Virus) âš ï¸ MAIN
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Non-pathogenic, non-integrating (mostly)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Capacity: ~4.7 kb
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Long-term expression in non-dividing
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ FDA-approved therapies exist
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 11.1.2 Lentivirus
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Integrating (stable but risky)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Capacity: ~8 kb
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Ex vivo preferred
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Good for dividing cells
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ 11.1.3 Adenovirus
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ High capacity (~36 kb)
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Strong immune response
â”‚   â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Transient expression
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Vaccine platform (COVID-19)
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ 11.1.4 Comparison
â”‚       Vector    â”‚ Capacity â”‚ Integration â”‚ Immunity â”‚ Duration
â”‚       â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
â”‚       AAV       â”‚ 4.7 kb   â”‚ Rare        â”‚ Low      â”‚ Long
â”‚       Lenti     â”‚ 8 kb     â”‚ Yes         â”‚ Low      â”‚ Stable
â”‚       Adeno     â”‚ 36 kb    â”‚ No          â”‚ High     â”‚ Short
